<div id="review_507957762" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/507957762" />
    <a title="Ash Wednesday" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10484016-ash-wednesday"><img alt="Ash Wednesday" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1379043440p2/10484016.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/507957762?book_show_action=true">Jan 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ash Wednesday" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ash Wednesday" href="/user/show/10484016-ash-wednesday">Ash Wednesday</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">people who've NEVER read a romance novel</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=cliches">cliches</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=bajillionaires">bajillionaires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=on-going-series">on-going-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=review">review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=i-m-gonna-be-in-the-minority">i-m-gonna-be-in-the-minority</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer507957762" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10084007313965754577">I'm having a hard time composing my thoughts because seriously, WTF did I just read?!<br/><br/>And Jesus, its going to be a series?! <br/><br/>Okay, coming into these kinds of books, you have certain expectations. I expect a serious amount of fluff and aww-shucks-ain't-that-sweet moments, drama is also requisite (some jealousy-induced punching, some crying in the rain), parties where everyone dresses up, non-graphic sex with dirrrrty talk... you know the usual. This book had everything and our backyard in there. Al</span>
  <span id="freeText10084007313965754577" style="display:none">I'm having a hard time composing my thoughts because seriously, WTF did I just read?!<br><br>And Jesus, its going to be a series?! <br><br>Okay, coming into these kinds of books, you have certain expectations. I expect a serious amount of fluff and aww-shucks-ain't-that-sweet moments, drama is also requisite (some jealousy-induced punching, some crying in the rain), parties where everyone dresses up, non-graphic sex with dirrrrty talk... you know the usual. This book had everything and our backyard in there. All the possible permutations of all the cliches we've read in contemporary romance smacks you in the face. All the reasons why it should've worked. And yet...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405381ra/789579.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The root of all fail in this book is the dialogue. It's too... fictional. <br><br><b> "Words fail to describe the way you look this evening." (Gavin)<br><br> Emily smiled sheepishly. "Thank you," she breathed out, grasping onto her clutch. "You look great <br> too."<br><br> "Why thank you." He smiled. "Shall we?" </b><br><br>Who are these people and why do they talk like that?! Also,<br><br><b> "Ah, yes, brother-in-law, take all the credit." Melanie laughed, tossing blonde hair over her shoulder. </b><br><br>WTF? Who calls their brother-in-law 'brother-in-law' to their face? And it's everywhere! Characters calling their friend, brother, sister, pal etc. as 'friend, pal, brother, sister'. It drove me crazy!<br><br><b> "Care to dance with the woman who brought you into this world?" </b> <br><br>That was Trevor and Gavin's mom asking Trevor to dance with him. Yikes.<br><br>Then there were the characters. The only character who I liked was Dillon. The supposed anti-hero was the only person in this story who reflected believable emotions and reactions for every situation he was in. And yes, he's still a douchebag but then that was the role he was meant to play.<br><br>Unlike Gavin, who I'm supposed to swoon over but dear Lord, that guy just cheesed me off. Actually my dislike of him was mostly still rooted to the way he talks:<br><br><b> "You're playing with fire man." (Trevor) "I can handle the burn. Just do what I asked. (Gavin)" </b><br><br>Ladies, that for you is your hero, Gavin Blake.<br><br>But far be it the only thing that will deter me from going Team Dillon all the way (actually I'm not team anything but humor me). No see, Gavin had a former flame by the name of Gina who makes an appearance somewhere in the middle of all this insanity. So they had a bitter past and you know how he handles a certain situation with her? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ He was so angry. Fuming mad. He wanted to throw her out but can't since she was so drunk. Then he dreams about her giving him head.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> And I'm supposed to root for this guy?! Gavin (and the author) obviously hadn't heard the adage that the opposite of love isn't hate but indifference because if he's seriously in love with Emily, that wouldn't have been the tone of that conversation. And what was up with that dream? Will that bite him in the ass ever? Because there was not one mention of it afterwards.<br><br>Emilie will probably get the brunt of the readers' hatred because she really was unbearably foolish and for me, evil. To actually <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ go back and marry Dillon because she thought Gavin was sleeping with Gina without plans of telling him even when he flat out asked  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> is such a dick thing to do. <br><br>Can a girl be a dick? Because having all this drama after your mom died not too long ago and nothing but so much as a glance referencing that supposedly painful moment. Yeah, Emilie's a dick.<br><br>The blurb has so much promise and the emotional depth that it could've gone to seemed obvious but the author didn't take it there. But everyone else seems to like this so what do I know anyway? Maybe not calling my mom "the woman who brought me into this world" in casual conversation is actually weird.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="10084007313965754577" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer599666125" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11461989350014053481"><b> 5 INFURIATING STARS </b> <br/><b>Collide </b> By <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6860574.Gail_McHugh' rel='nofollow noopener'>Gail McHugh</a><br/><b>Genres:</b> Contemporary Romance/Drama<br/><br/><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=saxht0' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311464i/688415.jpg' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Collide is a love story. It's a story about a girl called <b>Emily Cooper</b> . Emily moves to New York City with her boyfriend <b>Dillon Parker</b>, Dillon takes care of Emily, he provides everything she needs and especially after her mother's death, he was there for her, emotionally and financially! and she loves him...<br/><br/>Then she meets <b>Gavin Blake</b> New York most eligible bachelor, he's sexy, smart,and charming as hell! At the ti</span>
  <span id="freeText11461989350014053481" style="display:none"><b> 5 INFURIATING STARS </b> <br><b>Collide </b> By <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6860574.Gail_McHugh" rel="nofollow noopener">Gail McHugh</a><br><b>Genres:</b> Contemporary Romance/Drama<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=saxht0" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311464i/688415.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Collide is a love story. It's a story about a girl called <b>Emily Cooper</b> . Emily moves to New York City with her boyfriend <b>Dillon Parker</b>, Dillon takes care of Emily, he provides everything she needs and especially after her mother's death, he was there for her, emotionally and financially! and she loves him...<br><br>Then she meets <b>Gavin Blake</b> New York most eligible bachelor, he's sexy, smart,and charming as hell! At the time she didn't realize that<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[he was her boyfriend's best friend  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and when she meets him "officially " her feelings are not certain anymore, she's confused , unhappy,and turned on!<br>As the story goes we see how Dillon treats her, and how Gavin treats her. We also see her feelings are not the same for her boyfriend anymore and we also see how her feelings Evolve towards Gavin. <br><b> Will she choose Gavin Blake or Dillon Parker at the end ? </b><br><br><b>Will Dillon even allow her to make the choice or he'll force her in to choosing him? </b><br>Will if you really want to know then read the book ;) <br><br><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=saxht0" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311464i/688415.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><u> My Feelings Toward The Book </u><br><br>I honestly hated this book! yeah yeah 5 stars and all. I hated it because i was angry most of it. I mean Emily is stupid pushover !! if you are not happy with someone then DUMP HIM. Maybe she couldn't i'll give her that, you see Dillon is a dick with a capital D he's cruel and asshole, he treats her like a trophy, if he said jump she'll say how high????<br>Olivia &gt; Emily's friend Hates him and he hates her, she always telling her how ass he's being to her(Emily) then emily jumps to defend him by saying "oh no he's not, he sweet ohhhh i love him " <br>Bitch give me a break!!!<br>He helped her financially as i said earlier when her mother's death and also when she moved to new york BUT he won't let her forget it!! <br>what the fuck dude?! <br>The only reason she's with him is because she feels obligated to stay, and she feels that she owes him something! No darling you do not!<br><br>The Ending : <b>wHAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAT ??<br>NOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOO? OMG ... did he just? ohhhhh yes he did !!! <br>YEAHHHH YOU GO GIRL</b><br>------<br><br>lets talk tiny little bit about the cover: who is the idiot who made this!!!?? ugly, stupid, irrelevant!!! <br><br><br><u> The Characters </u><br><br><b>Gavin Blake:</b> *blush* he's just ASDFGHJKL LOVED HIM , sweet, nice , sexy , smart and hot! am i missing something here Emily?<br><br><b>Emily:</b> liked her but darling any man touches me the wrong way and i'll break his arm! not to mention <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[forcing you to have sex with him ( one of the last scenes  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> oh HELL No! UGH i'm angry at her.<br><b>Dillon Parker</b>: I didn't know at which point i KNEW he was a dick but thank god it was from the very beginning.<br><b>his mother</b>: PLASTIC BITCH can someone slap her?<br><br><b>Olivia</b> : LOVED HER, seems my kind of girl.<br><br><b>Fallen? is that her name? anyway loved her also <br>There are a number of the characters and i liked them all </b><br><br><br>Some Quotes i liked : <br><br><i>"Her heart beg an t o race like a frightened little mouse fleeing its predator.<br>Dillon pulled his chair away from the table.<br>Thump…<br>Dillon slowly got down on one knee.<br>Thump…thump…<br>Dillon produced a small black velvet box .<br>Thump….<br>Thump….<br>Flat line….<br>Beeeeeeeeeeep…" </i><br><br><br><br><i>"“Sometimes bad choices bring us to the<br>right people .”</i><br><br><i>"“Here's to bottle caps,the Yankees, and 'birds', and most of all"...he paused and lowered his voice to a whisper.." and,most of all to a beautiful girl named Molly who refuses to believe the man-the man who loves her more than she'll ever know” </i><br><br><br><i> “Every part of you was made for me. Your lips were made to kiss mine, your eyes were made to wake up to me looking at you in my bed every morning, and your fucking tongue was made to roll my name off of it. I am more certain of us than I'm certain that I require oxygen to breathe.” </i><br><br><br><i> “ I've never felt so heartbroken and so in love at the same time. If you would've told me the day we met that you were going to break my heart— and that days, months, or even years would pass, that I would still be hurting like this—it wouldn't have stopped me from falling in love with you.” </i><br><br><i>“With the weight of his body, he pressed her back against the wall, and licked the soft spot below her earlobe. "Tell me how much you fucking want me," he breathed.” </i><br><br><i>“Don’t we all have to fill voids in our lives with something?” </i><br><br><i>“When you want something this badly, you don't just give up. <div id="review_483664726" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/483664726" />
    <a title="Bookhooking (Tanya Witt)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4940504-bookhooking-tanya-witt"><img alt="Bookhooking (Tanya Witt)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1415114133p2/4940504.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/483664726?book_show_action=true">Dec 23, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bookhooking (Tanya Witt)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bookhooking (Tanya Witt)" href="/user/show/4940504-bookhooking-tanya-witt">Bookhooking (Tanya Witt)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4940504-bookhooking-tanya-witt?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4940504-bookhooking-tanya-witt?shelf=highly-recommended">highly-recommended</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4940504-bookhooking-tanya-witt?shelf=arc-for-review">arc-for-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4940504-bookhooking-tanya-witt?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4940504-bookhooking-tanya-witt?shelf=review-request-from-author">review-request-from-author</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer483664726" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17977329736139175025">Holy hell of a good story here! If I could give it more than five stars I most definitely would!! Gail McHugh introduced me to my first book boyfriend of 2013 and his name is none other than Gavin Blake!!<p>Oh my, how I adored him in every f***ing way! She had my undivided attention from the first page until the very last and let me just say that it takes a pretty, awesome author to do that to me because I can get easily distracted, but here? oh hell no there was none of that happening! I didn't wa</p></span>
  <span id="freeText17977329736139175025" style="display:none">Holy hell of a good story here! If I could give it more than five stars I most definitely would!! Gail McHugh introduced me to my first book boyfriend of 2013 and his name is none other than Gavin Blake!!<p>Oh my, how I adored him in every f***ing way! She had my undivided attention from the first page until the very last and let me just say that it takes a pretty, awesome author to do that to me because I can get easily distracted, but here? oh hell no there was none of that happening! I didn't want to go to bed, I didn't want to eat dinner, and I didn't even want to go to the bathroom!! okay okay so you want me to tell you WHY I loved this book so much well that is easy and I can even sum it up in TWO words yep that's right only TWO words....GAVIN BLAKE!!</p><p><br />This wonderful man captured my heart and my soul and even totally aside from this: Emily's description of him<br /><br /><b>"Yes, he was that good looking. Take-your-breath-away good looking. Want -to-strip-your-body-naked-and-let-him-devour-you-alive good looking. Certified-eye-candy good looking."</b><br /><br />Okay I had my Gavin moment so now we move on to Dillon, Emily, Trevor, Olivia &amp; Fallon. I will start with Emily, oh my dear Emily such a, how do you say, somewhat likable but difficult character and at the very same time I understood her.</p><p> She has lost her mother and throughout all of the devastation that took place with that, Dillon, her boyfriend, was there to see her through it all, to take care of her, take care of the funeral expenses and arrangements, you name it, he did it making Emily forever indebted to him, at least in her mind. I personally didn't like Dillon from the get go, I don't care what he did, and for very good reason!!</p><p>After that emotional roller coaster was over Emily moved to New York where Dillon lived although she wasn't ready to move in with him just yet, (I am secretly thanking God here) she decided to room with her friend Olivia and I just loved Olivia!! She made me smile more than once especially when she said<br /><br /><b>"I'm about to drop it like it's hot."</b><br /><br />referring to snooty tooty Joan, Dillon's mother.</p><p><br />Once Emily moves to New York she finds a job at a restaurant where she meets Fallon and they also become friends. One evening there was a delivery to be made and no delivery man so Emily took on that role and that is when her world would completely change and she would collide with<b> HIM</b>!</p><p>Gavin's attraction to Emily is instant and completely overwhelming to him in every way. After there encounter he decides to pursues her only to discover she has a boyfriend but will that change anything? Does he continue to pursue her? why yes, yes he does and let me just quote this for you and then you can decide for yourself what Emily should do...<br /><br /><b>"I want you more than I've ever wanted anything before in my f***ing life."</b><br /><br /><b>"I could've f***ed you over... and over...and over again, and I could've f***ed you very well, but I stopped because that's not the way I wanted you."</b><br /><br />Holy hell does my man have a heart and got it all going on or what? I could go on and on about how much I loved this book! There is Drama with a capital D, there is angst, sex, love, frustration, torment, lies, and emotional, heart and gut wrenching pain but oh so completely and utterly worth every bit of it!! (I only wanted to throw my kindle once lol)</p><p>The last quote I will leave you with because I was a highlighting queen let me tell you.<br /><br /><b>He was everything she wanted, and apparently, she was nothing he needed.</b><br /><br />So what will Emily do? Will she stay with Dillon or will she let go and give herself to Gavin?</p><p>I was provided an ARC of this by the author, Gail McHugh, for an honest review and for this I truly, truly thank her because she is one talented lady and I can't wait for the day she makes the NYT'S bestseller's list and I can say I read her books before they made it here!!! Do yourselves a favor and BUY this book because I truly believe you will not be sorry and you WILL want more!!</p></span>
  <a data-text-id="17977329736139175025" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1078958860" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1078958860" />
    <a title="Ramona Popescu " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/33526516-ramona-popescu"><img alt="Ramona Popescu " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594649997p2/33526516.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1078958860?book_show_action=true">Oct 13, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ramona Popescu " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ramona Popescu " href="/user/show/33526516-ramona-popescu">Ramona Popescu </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=hot-romance">hot-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=love-this-series">love-this-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=man-crush">man-crush</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1078958860" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18056733042851199274">This is one of the most wonderful books in 2015 and although it has a lot of controversy around it, I loved it.<br/><br/>This is a story about betrayal and suffering, but also one about love and second chances.<br/>The main plot surrounds Emily Cooper who begins a new life in NY together with her boyfriend, Dillon. In the first chapters we see a happy couple,that is trying to settle down and enjoy their relationship. <br/><br/>Dillon was there for Emily in her terrible moments of grief and due to all the background they</span>
  <span id="freeText18056733042851199274" style="display:none">This is one of the most wonderful books in 2015 and although it has a lot of controversy around it, I loved it.<br><br>This is a story about betrayal and suffering, but also one about love and second chances.<br>The main plot surrounds Emily Cooper who begins a new life in NY together with her boyfriend, Dillon. In the first chapters we see a happy couple,that is trying to settle down and enjoy their relationship. <br><br>Dillon was there for Emily in her terrible moments of grief and due to all the background they have, this start means much to them in order to make their relation permanent. Emily's world will be shook once Gavin enters the scene. He is a charming business man, friend of Dillon's, who finds Emily fascinating. The fact that he is funny, handsome and has a lot of things in common with her helps them develop a sweet friendship. I will not spoil everything about how they met, you will have to read the book and believe in destiny:)<br><br>Things progress in a natural manner, Emily's path intersected with Gavin's many times and in all of them we can see how different he is from Dillon. The antithesis between them is obvious at a point and everyone can see it, including Emily. While Gavin is sweet, attentive and caring, Dillon is frustrating, mean, bored and sometimes even violent. <br><br>I like the awareness the writer sends here regarding domestic violence, an often element inserted in book with a certain purpose. Slowly a love triangle is formed but there were circumstances regarding the events that went on. <br><br>Emily's and Dillon relationship is based on domination from Dillon's side, no tenderness, respect and apparently no love. In opposition to that, Gavin loves Emily sincerely and will do anything to make her happy, he fights for her and he is determined to show her how great they can be together. A lot of mistakes are made by Emily because she wanted to do the right thing, but sometimes destiny has other plans for you.<br><br>This book had one of the most intense love scenes I have ever read, without being too much, too exaggerated. It had the right amount of love, sensuality and passion that needed to be included in the book, and made the scenes look fantastic and hot. That intensity was felt not only in the love scenes, but also in the relationship between Emily and Gavin, all their dialogues, their glimpses, their attraction were so beautifully described and made you connect with them.<br><br>Many will ask if cheating is involved and well, I am going to let you discover that by yourself because many have the tendency of judging before actually understanding the circumstances leading to a certain outcome. But please, be open minded and put yourself in Emily's place. The heroine was very well developed and you will certain connect with her in all emotional levels. Put yourself in her position and try to see what you would have done in her place. From my point of view, the answer isn't that hard. <br><br>Maybe she did a lot of mistakes, but being confused and scare never helps anybody make the right decision. In the end, it is never too late to realize that maybe you choose wrong and if a thing was made for you, you will have it eventually. <br>That is what Collide is all about- making the right decision based on what you need and dream about, and having the courage to seek it, even if you are not convinced that all odds are in your favor. <br><br>5 stars and definitely one of my favorites!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479123324i/21149668._SX540_.png" width="500" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more reviews please check <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://readwithloveblog.wordpress.com">https://readwithloveblog.wordpress.com</a> </span>
  <a data-text-id="18056733042851199274" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_484504891" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/484504891" />
    <a title="E.L. Montes" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13035872-e-l-montes"><img alt="E.L. Montes" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442643730p2/13035872.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/484504891?book_show_action=true">Dec 24, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="E.L. Montes" class="user" itemprop="url" name="E.L. Montes" href="/user/show/13035872-e-l-montes">E.L. Montes</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer484504891" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15617732317368213682">I was given Collide as an ARC by the author in exchange for an honest review.<br/><br/>4 ½ Beautiful Colliding Stars!<br/><br/>After the devastating death in her family, Emily Cooper made the ultimate decision to start new and fresh, by leaving her small town and joining her boyfriend, Dillon Parker, in New York City. Even though this was a huge step in their relationship Emily wasn’t quite ready to live with Dillon and therefore moved in with her best friend Olivia.<br/><br/>While trying to cope with the loss, Emily began l</span>
  <span id="freeText15617732317368213682" style="display:none">I was given Collide as an ARC by the author in exchange for an honest review.<br /><br />4 ½ Beautiful Colliding Stars!<br /><br />After the devastating death in her family, Emily Cooper made the ultimate decision to start new and fresh, by leaving her small town and joining her boyfriend, Dillon Parker, in New York City. Even though this was a huge step in their relationship Emily wasn’t quite ready to live with Dillon and therefore moved in with her best friend Olivia.<br /><br />While trying to cope with the loss, Emily began living her life and even found a small job as a waitress at an Italian restaurant. On the first day of her new job, the delivery boy quit, so she was asked by her boss if she could make a quick delivery to a building nearby.<br />This is when we meet: GAVIN BLAKE.<br /><br />Attracting, compelling, colliding, their chemistry - to say the least - was explosive. He felt it the first time he laid eyes on her, the drawing of energy that radiated from her eyes as she stared into his.<br /><br />Let me tell you something about Gavin Blake. He is up there in my top five book boyfriends. Want to know why? Gavin was the perfect mix of Gideon Cross and Kellan Kyle. I know right! How could you NOT fall in love with a man that’s a mixture of your two ULTIMATE book boyfriends! (Well my two ultimate book bf). He had the power and wealth as Gideon. Though, his personality is what won me over. Slightly similar to Kellan, but he was his own character within himself. He wasn’t controlling, over possessive, and domineering. He was gorgeous, smart, humorous, charming, and the list could go on. His connection with Emily was STRONG and I knew the moment they laid eyes on each other he was in for the biggest fight of his life.<br /><br />My heart tore into pieces watching Emily struggle with her feelings of what she thought might be for Gavin and the feelings for her current boyfriend, Dillon. I wanted to smack some sense into her because it was clear SO clear. There were other times I wanted to hug her and tell her “I know it’s hard! I’m sorry you’re going through this, but go with your heart!” But THEN I wanted to slap the living days out of her AGAIN.<br /><br />Collide will take you on an emotional, devastating, yet delicious, love-triangle of a roller coaster. It will be a ride that you will not want to get off. Be prepared though, you’ll want to rip your hair out, scream, love, hug your kindle, and shout some more.<br />The ending left me screaming at my tablet, “NOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOO!” But I’m ready for what Gail McHugh has to offer with these characters in “Pulse” the sequel to Collide.<br /><br />Loved this book! It’ll be released January 20, 2013. Grabs yours ASAP.<br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15617732317368213682" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/487799324?book_show_action=true">Dec 28, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog">Smitten&#39;s Book Blog</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=angst-filled-reads">angst-filled-reads</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=steamy-reads">steamy-reads</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer487799324" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2266025090928067711"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402378i/782060._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402378i/782061._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>OH MYYYYY LIFE!<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402378i/782062._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Ok, I'm going to start off with a warning. Only read this book when you have bugger all else to do for the day! You will not want to put it down!<br/><br/>Jesus, what a rollercoaster! This book has totally messed up my day. I read last night until I physically could not keep my eyes open. I was so tired that I was falling asleep half way through a chapter and dreaming the rest of the story. In the end, I gave up. I picked it up when the other half left for work and said to myself 'Oh, I'll </span>
  <span id="freeText2266025090928067711" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402378i/782060._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402378i/782061._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>OH MYYYYY LIFE!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402378i/782062._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ok, I'm going to start off with a warning. Only read this book when you have bugger all else to do for the day! You will not want to put it down!<br><br>Jesus, what a rollercoaster! This book has totally messed up my day. I read last night until I physically could not keep my eyes open. I was so tired that I was falling asleep half way through a chapter and dreaming the rest of the story. In the end, I gave up. I picked it up when the other half left for work and said to myself 'Oh, I'll just read a bit before I get up.' Two hours later and I drag myself out of bed to feed my poor starving dogs. <br>Whilst eating my breakfast, I decide to just read a bit before getting in the shower and continuing with my day. That was two hours ago. And here I sit, unshowered, in my PJs, breakfast bowl on the table next to me, writing this review!!! I couldn't not! I had to get it out.<br><br>So, let's talk about <i>Collide</i>. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402378i/782063.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Wow. It's intense! Who did I love and who did I hate... I loved Gavin, my feelings yo-yo'd for Emily and <i>hated</i> Dillon!!! There are great surrounding characters in this book too. Emily's friend's Olivia and Fallon are fab. Gavin's friend Trevor is super cute.<br><br>In <i>Collide</i> Emily moves to New York to be nearer her boyfriend, Dillon, and best friend, Olivia, after the death of her mother. But upon moving into the post-college 'real world' and what is also Dillon's world, things aren't what Emily hopes they will be. <br>Dillon's high powered job keeps him out late at night, his interfering exes rear their ugly heads, his alcohol consumption seems to be spiralling out of control and he has a temper that Emily hadn't witnessed before.<br>And to top it all off, Emily meets Gavin. Gavin is insanely sexy. He's gorgeous, wealthy, charming and he's got his heart set on Emily.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Though his father had told him stories about it happening, until that fateful afternoon, Gavin Blake had believed that love at first site didn't exist.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>And then they realise that Gavin is Dillon's close friend and Emily is Dillon's girlfriend. <i>Collide</i> follows Gavin and Emily as they try to deal with their undeniable connection to one another and the fallout that it leaves in it's wake. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I've never felt so heartbroken and so in love at the same time. If you would've told me the day we met that you were going to break my heart - and that days, months, or even years would pass, that I would still be hurting like this - it wouldn't have stopped me from falling in love with you."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402378i/782064.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>We'll begin with Emily. Urgh, the girl needed a kick up the backside at times. I didn't dislike her. At times my heart broke for her. At times I wanted to shake her. And at times I was right behind her, cheering her on. Dillon helped her through an incredibly painful time, when she lost her mother and she feels strongly indebted to him for this. I can completely see why this drives some of her poor choices and reactions to his behaviour. But, my God, was it frustrating!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Her mind tried to fight a bloody battle against what her body already knew. She wanted him, and she wanted him bad.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Dillon is a dickhead. There's no two ways about it. He's controlling, possessive, aggressive, arrogant, manipulative, disrespectful, unfaithful, dishonest... shall I continue?! I absolutely hated him from quite early on in the book. As soon as he started becoming a little overbearing, I could totally see where the author was taking the story and my dislike for Dillon began to fester. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402378i/782065.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And then there's Gavin. *sigh* Gavin Gavin Gavin Gavin Gavin. <i>
  <b>'Mr. Tall, Dark and Fuckable Handsome'</b>
</i>! At the beginning of the book, he's just undeniably hot, smooth, panty-wetting, gorgeous, [insert complimentary adjective here]... But as the book progresses, he becomes so much more than that. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402378i/782066._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now, I'm not usually one to buy into the whole 'love at first sight' spiel, but it totally didn't bother me in this book. I luuurrrved the way Gavin wanted Emily. I loved that every time they were in the same room, their eyes locked and they were drawn to one another. I loved that he felt that she was meant to be with him, despite the fact that she was with Dillon. And, hell, I was even bouncing in my seat when they were sneaking around behind everyone's backs!! The stolen touches, the secret glances, the whispered innuendos. Mmmmm mmmm!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Am I making it hard for you?" he asked mockingly.<br>"Yes, Gavin you are," she quietly spat, her fingertips white-knuckled around her glass. <br>With his need for her trapped inside - blistering hot, sweltering, ready to explode - he leaned in closer, dropping his voice. "Good, because whenever you're near me, I fucking lose every bit of self-control I have left."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Speaking of which... Oh my goodness, this book is Haaaawt! with a capital H and an 'aw'! <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"There's not a man on Earth who doesn't wish he was me right now. Your mind and your body will never forget the things I'm going to do to you tonight. Every...single...inch of your body is going to feel me."<br>"Oh my God."<br>"Yes."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I guess it's the idea of the forbidden fruit. The taboo. And I know it makes me a very bad, morally corrupt person, but squeeeee, I freakin' loved it! It's like Thoughtless, but if Denny were a complete tool!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I want you to give in to what I see behind your eyes every time I'm near you. I want you to give in to the way you trembled in my arms when I touched you... the way your breathing becomes faster when I look at you. I loved the way your lips felt against mine, and I'm pretty sure you did, too. I also enjoy the way I can almost feel you becoming wet for me right now. Are you going to pretend that you don't feel anything for me, Emily?"</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402378i/782067.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And lastly, there's the ending. Jesus H. Christ! I've had this on my Kindle for months and I kept looking at it, wondering if I should just read it. And then I got asked to be a part of the blog tour to read and review the second book, <i>Pulse</i>. So, I decided to put <i>Collide</i> on hold and wait until near the date of my blog stop, so that I could read both at once. Thank fuck I did! Otherwise, right now, I'd be pulling my hair out. It's a brutal, heart-pounding, palm-sweating cliffhanger. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Sometimes, bad choices bring us to the right people."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402378i/782068._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The last 20% of this book is fast paced and absolutely deliciously juicy! I couldn't tear my eyes away (hence the lack of shower debacle). It's steamy, heart breaking, intense, painful and explosive. <br><br>So, I'm going to force myself to go and do normal day-to-day, mandatory things right now, before allowing myself to dive into Pulse ready for my blog spot on Monday. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402378i/782069._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b><i>Collide</i> Statistics</b><br><b>Steam Rating (out of 5):</b> ♥♥♥♥♥<br><b>Ending:</b> Cliffhanger<br><b>Series:</b> ✓ (<i>Collide</i> series)<br><b>Reading Order:</b><br>Book #1 - <i>Collide</i><br>Book #2 - <i>Pulse</i><br><b>Can this be read as a standalone?</b> No<br><b>Themes:</b><br>Love triangle<br>Love at first sight<br>Controlling partner<br><b>Warning. This book includes... </b><br>Love triangle<br>Love at first sight<br>Controlling partner<br>Cheating<br><b>Writing:</b> Great<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389732917i/8051747._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389732917i/8051748._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>UK AMAZON: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.co.uk/Collide-Volume-1-ebook/dp/B00B385VCU/ref=sr_1_1?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1374665685&amp;sr=8-1&amp;keywords=collide+gail+mchugh">http://www.amazon.co.uk/Collide-Volum...</a><br>US AMAZON: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.com/Collide-Volume-1-ebook/dp/B00B385VCU/ref=sr_1_1?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1374665685&amp;sr=8-1&amp;keywords=collide+gail+mchugh">http://www.amazon.com/Collide-Volume-...</a><br><br><b>

    <a title="Maribel  Giusto " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4061385-maribel-giusto"><img alt="Maribel  Giusto " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505234021p2/4061385.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/485970877?book_show_action=true">Dec 26, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maribel  Giusto " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maribel  Giusto " href="/user/show/4061385-maribel-giusto">Maribel  Giusto </a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4061385-maribel-giusto?shelf=delectable-dudes">delectable-dudes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4061385-maribel-giusto?shelf=book-boyfraannn">book-boyfraannn</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4061385-maribel-giusto?shelf=beautifully-broken-leading-chickie">beautifully-broken-leading-chickie</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer485970877" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8319997248501627354"><i>I received an ARC copy from the author in exchange for an honest review...</i><br/><br/><b>4.5 Stars!! Collide is Freaking Phenomenal!</b> <br/><br/>I'm so glad that this was the book to start off my 2013! I love the way Gail McHugh writes! Her prose is so smooth, the story flowed seamlessly. I think one of my favorite things about this book was the fact that there was so much raw emotion that bled from its pages. <br/><br/><a href='http://smg.beta.photobucket.com/user/Tinker526/media/collideEm1_zps926e6125.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402113i/781413.jpg' alt='Emily-Collide' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Emily: Her character developed beautifully. Broken, but hanging on to the things she holds dear. Her boyfrien</span>
  <span id="freeText8319997248501627354" style="display:none"><i>I received an ARC copy from the author in exchange for an honest review...</i><br><br><b>4.5 Stars!! Collide is Freaking Phenomenal!</b> <br><br>I'm so glad that this was the book to start off my 2013! I love the way Gail McHugh writes! Her prose is so smooth, the story flowed seamlessly. I think one of my favorite things about this book was the fact that there was so much raw emotion that bled from its pages. <br><br><a href="http://smg.beta.photobucket.com/user/Tinker526/media/collideEm1_zps926e6125.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402113i/781413.jpg" alt="Emily-Collide" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Emily: Her character developed beautifully. Broken, but hanging on to the things she holds dear. Her boyfriend, her sister, her best-friend Olivia, and her boyfriend Dillon. Things seem to be coming together, until.....(enter incredibly, painfully gorgeous, dreamy, fu*kable, amazing, charming Gavin.)<br><br><a href="http://smg.beta.photobucket.com/user/Tinker526/media/collideGav3_zps949e5cea-1_zps8dcb5d2f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402113i/781414._SX540_.jpg" alt="collideGav3_zps949e5cea" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Gavin: Like seriously... where is the machine that turns our book boyfriends into flesh because I am completely head over heels in love with this <i>delectable dude</i>! Gavin Blake is just ...Wow! They way he loves is stunning. The things that he makes Emily feel *sigh*....Fate definitely had a good time with these two, and it will have you holding your breath, jaw dropping to the floor,and smiling like a fool! <br><br><a href="http://smg.beta.photobucket.com/user/Tinker526/media/collideEmGav1_zpsdc134eba.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402113i/781415._SX540_.jpg" alt="collideEmGav1_zpsdc134eba" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Collide is the total package, steamy, fun, and a little heart-wrenching. Gail does a wonderful job at making you feel like you are part of everything that's going on throughout the whole book. By the end, if you don't already feel like you know the characters personally, you may need to re-read it 'cause you definitely missed something. Her characters are as real as they come.<br><br>So I said all of that, just to say this.... <b>Mark your friggin' Calendars!! for January 21,2013!!!This WILL be one of your favorite reads, I'm sure of it!</b> <br><br><br> <br> <a href="http://smg.beta.photobucket.com/user/Tinker526/media/collide-BC_zpsd56ca4a0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402113i/781416._SX540_.jpg" alt="collide-BC_zpsd56ca4a0" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer512851779" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer9223634400467375368">Oh boy, I don't even know where to start. I had high hopes for this book but it definitely fell short for me. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391822252ra/8461644.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Emily has moved to New York to be closer to her boyfriend, Dillon. She moves in with her best friend from college, Olivia. Olivia was one of my favorite characters. She was hilarious.<br/><br/>I never had a good feeling about Dillon, he was a complete douchebag. He was horrible to Emily and always made it out to be Emily's fault.<br/><br/>Enter Gavin, the one good thing about this whole book.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380408862ra/800150.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>He meets Emily </span>
  <span id="freeText9223634400467375368" style="display:none">Oh boy, I don't even know where to start. I had high hopes for this book but it definitely fell short for me. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391822252ra/8461644.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Emily has moved to New York to be closer to her boyfriend, Dillon. She moves in with her best friend from college, Olivia. Olivia was one of my favorite characters. She was hilarious.<br><br>I never had a good feeling about Dillon, he was a complete douchebag. He was horrible to Emily and always made it out to be Emily's fault.<br><br>Enter Gavin, the one good thing about this whole book.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380408862ra/800150.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>He meets Emily on a chance encounter as she is delivering his food from the restaurant where she works. They have an immediate attraction to each other. Gavin is in hot pursuit.......until he meets his friend Dillon and his girlfriend at a club and all hopes of having Emily comes crashing down around him. <br><br><br><b>
  <i>"Sometimes bad choices bring us to the right people, Emily."</i>
</b><br><br><br>Gavin knows that Dillon isn't treating Emily the way she deserves to be treated. She might be dating his friend, but that doesn't keep him from wanting her. For now he has decided to just be her friend. They have a very strong sexual chemistry but they also develop a very good friendship.<br><br>When things comes crashing down in Emily's world, Gavin is there to pick her up.<br><br><br><b>
  <i>"When you want something this badly, you don't just give up. You fight and fight until you absolutely can't fight anymore."</i>
</b> ~Gavin<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391822252i/8461645._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>The reason I didn't like this book was basically all due to Emily. She was very fickle, indecisive, and an all around pain in my ass. </span>

<div id="review_483413785" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/483413785" />
    <a title="Kim Person" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7590856-kim-person"><img alt="Kim Person" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1434694589p2/7590856.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/483413785?book_show_action=true">Dec 22, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kim Person" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kim Person" href="/user/show/7590856-kim-person">Kim Person</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7590856-kim-person?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer483413785" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2805258221367696937">I was provide an arc in exchange for an honest review of Gail's Collide and I have to say in the end it was I who is extremely honored that she blessed me with a copy of this book!<br/><br/>If I could this would be rated TEN HOLY MOTHER GIVE ME MORE NOW STARS!! I was Stunned, shredded and left speechless at the end of the book but I'm absolutely in love with Collide!! <br/><br/>This is the story of Emily who moves from Colorado to NYC with the encouragement of her boyfriend Dillon. Emily has graduated college and m</span>
  <span id="freeText2805258221367696937" style="display:none">I was provide an arc in exchange for an honest review of Gail's Collide and I have to say in the end it was I who is extremely honored that she blessed me with a copy of this book!<br><br>If I could this would be rated TEN HOLY MOTHER GIVE ME MORE NOW STARS!! I was Stunned, shredded and left speechless at the end of the book but I'm absolutely in love with Collide!! <br><br>This is the story of Emily who moves from Colorado to NYC with the encouragement of her boyfriend Dillon. Emily has graduated college and moves in with her best friend and college roommate Olivia. Emily met Dillon when Olivia's brother Trevor came and visited the girls one weekend while they were in college and the rest is history or is it?????<br><br>I must say I had NO clue what I was getting myself into when I started this one. I knew the synopsis and that was it. I refused to chat with anyone about the book until after I read it and well I started reading and it wasn't long before I was sitting in my chair doing this......<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401728ra/780077.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Emily gets to NYC and she needs a job and she promptly gets one as a waitress! She's leaving after her first shift and her boss Antonio asks that she drops off an order. Easy not a big deal and who knew that would be the first time Emily "collides" with the infamous Gavin Blake. I predict that you will fall in LOVE I mean head over heels in love with Gavin :) Who wouldn't millionaire, SINGLE, and schmexy as all get out. Yep, if I walked in and made instant eye contact with his ice blue eyes I would totally................<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401728ra/780078.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>This story is told in alternating POV which I LOVED! We had Emily POV and Gavin's. Gavin see's Emily and guess what - yep, this unattached player is hit right in the heart with cupid's arrow. But don't you dare for one minute think this is the "typical" player nope you will find Gavin is freaking ahhhhhh-ma-zing! Wait I almost forgot Dillon........<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401728ra/780079.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>But are they bad? or are they really really good ;) Well, this is one of those books that I seriously cannot give you too much of the plot line but I CAN and will give you some glimpses of the book through my eyes.............<br><br>You have Olivia who is bad arse and doesn't fancy Dillon at all her typical reaction when he walks in the room is....................<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380374773ra/729052.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Trevor he's a pretty cool dude and I really liked him but his like Switzerland when things start going down..........<br><br>I can't forget this................................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380862707ra/3138501.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I really wish I read this..............<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401728ra/780080.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Wait, was there?<br><br>In any event the relationships were complex and when I say relationships I don't mean just Dillon &amp; Emily. I mean everyone of the characters has some connection to something which really would screw with me too if I was Emily.<br><br>This book did pull every emotion from me. I went from ..........<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401728ra/780081.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Right on to.................................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380371663ra/724788.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>at times I was................................................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/679046.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>And then I got towards the end you know when there is enough left where you are crying one minute and you think ahhhhh I'm going to be okay. I was left going.........................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401728ra/780082.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh did I mention, there's another book? Oh yes my friends there is another one in the series! <br><br>In all seriousness this book is very well written. The amazing love scenes are described in such a way I've never read before that I wasn't reading the same 'ole thing. This is a MUST READ for 2013 and then you can sit back with me and wait for book two to see where this continues.<br><br>This book was like NOTHING I've read recently heck I can't recall reading a book with this plot line. It's one of those true gems that you read and when finish you literally are giddy and talking a mile a minute, yes I was to my spouse, but at the same time you are craving, dying and needing more, much, much more!<br><br>I'm seriously doing this over Gail McHugh.....................<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401729ra/780083.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Gail you ROCK! This is outstanding and I cannot wait to see everyone's reaction to this once it is released. I don't think there are enough adjectives for me to describe how I feel after reading this book!<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17158596.Collide" title="Collide by Gail McHugh" rel="nofollow noopener">Collide</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6860574.Gail_McHugh" title="Gail McHugh" rel="nofollow noopener">Gail McHugh</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="2805258221367696937" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog">Jenny - TotallybookedBlog</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer488020069" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5678455076942022220">I so wanted to love this book, I really did.<br/><br/>I did start out enjoying it. The opening couple of chapters hooked me in and I was feeling a connection to Emily as we join her in her move to New York where she is making a fresh start following the death of her mother.<br/><br/>These initial scenes drew me in and I was feeling for Emily at this point and thought, here it is, I’m going to love this girl and love this story. She’s independent, compassionate, sweet and came across quite strong at this juncture of</span>
  <span id="freeText5678455076942022220" style="display:none">I so wanted to love this book, I really did.<br /><br />I did start out enjoying it. The opening couple of chapters hooked me in and I was feeling a connection to Emily as we join her in her move to New York where she is making a fresh start following the death of her mother.<br /><br />These initial scenes drew me in and I was feeling for Emily at this point and thought, here it is, I’m going to love this girl and love this story. She’s independent, compassionate, sweet and came across quite strong at this juncture of the story.<br /><br />At this point we are also introduced to her boyfriend Dillon who comes across as loving, thoughtful and caring. He has been her rock during her mother’s illness and steered her through the days following her mother’s death. Dillon has been there for her. Attentively looking after her and visiting while she is at her mother’s bedside wherever possible. He’s by her side, but it’s what you would expect from a loving boyfriend.<br /><br />Emily is making a delivery the day she first encounters Gavin. There is a charge between these two. A connection they both feel that neither can deny. Gavin acknowledges it, Emily tries to dismiss it. After all, she is deeply in love with Dillon.<br /><br />I really did enjoy hearing both Gavin and Emily’s voices in this story and it enabled me to experience his instant attraction and the overall intense feelings he had for Emily that he couldn’t explain. He knew she felt them too but getting her to admit her feelings for him was going to take some work, but Gavin was prepared to do whatever was necessary to make Emily admit her feelings for him, feelings he knows they both share.<br /><br />Once Dillon is back on familiar territory he starts showing glimpses of the “real” Dillon. The real Dillon is very different to the Dillon we’ve been introduced to earlier on. <br />In fact the real Dillon is inconsiderate and pretty awful and herein lies my problem with how I started to disconnect form the story and the characters.<br /><br />As Dillon’s real personality flaws started to emerge so does his disrespect and unreasonable treatment of Emily start coming to the forefront. <br /><br />On the one hand we have Gavin. Gavin is the perfect guy. Handsome, kind, caring, wears his heart on his sleeve, a stoic millionaire playboy who doesn’t realise something’s missing in his life until he meets Emily. After having his heart broken some years earlier, he’s always been a bit gun shy of relationships and falling in love but after seeing Emily, he has feelings he thought he would never experience again.<br /><br />The decision on who to choose was simple really. Well, it was for me. Who do you choose?<br /><br />The cruel, manipulative awful Dillon or the wonderful, kind, caring, passionate, protective Gavin, who never ceases in his pursuit of her knowing that she felt the same way about him. <i> “Tell me how much you fucking want me”</i><br /><br />The fact that Emily had such a hard time deciding and flip flopping drove me crazy. I just didn’t get it. Yes, I understood that she felt she owed Dillon something for how he supported her through her Mum’s illness and passing and she was mindful that Gavin and Dillon were friends, if you could call them that.<br /><br />But for me, I really couldn’t grasp the extent she went to in her relationship with Dillon and how she disregarded all the signs that were right in front of her face.<br /><br />Emily would never listen to anyone but most of all she refused to hear Gavin out. <br />This frustrated me and I felt so sorry for Gavin who was so patient and he never shied from telling Emily how he felt<br /><i>“You belong with me, not him." Every part of you was made for me. Your lips were made to kiss mine, your eyes were made to wake up to me looking at you in my bed every morning, and your fucking tongue was made to roll my name off it. I am more certain of us than I'm certain that I require oxygen to breathe." </i><br /><br />Yes, he certainly let her know his feelings whereas Dillon seemed to provide her with nothing but heartache and confusion.<br /><br />Emily frustrated me to the point where I wanted to jump into my kindle and slap some sense into her and tell Gavin to run and never return and find happiness elsewhere, and the miscommunication over the ex girlfriend was irritating and and unbelievable.<br /><br />The over abundance of words stalled the story for me at times and I found some of the analogies a bit off putting too <i>"he licked thorugh the sweet juices as if he were savoring a popsicle on a hot summer day".</i><br /><br />I did however find myself wanting to know what happened and the ending has set up book two perfectly.<br /><br /><br /><i>An Arc was supplied by the author for an honest review </i></span>
  <a data-text-id="5678455076942022220" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('k7+VdGRdHIn9HMH75L8HvIHifqqHGuOe39/vXoVbvy6EnOBaJ1dfB9wKITlCeNWQxC3jWGj/20NFdhCBWplIAA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {

  }

  <span id="freeText9001091479941192342" style="display:none">A self-proclaimed chocoholic, married mother of three, and a lover of writing for as far back as she can remember, Gail McHugh is the author of two New York Times bestselling novels. The COLLIDE series (which includes COLLIDE and PULSE), was acquired by Atria Books on September 17th, 2013.<br /><br />“The first of two sexy contemporary romances about a woman torn between her seemingly perfect boyfriend and a dark, mysterious stranger who will stop at nothing to have her.” - Publishers Weekly on COLLIDE, a Top 10 Romance pick! <br /><br />Gail's next novel (also publishing through Atria Books), AMBER TO ASHES, is slated to release June 9th, 2015.<br /><br />You can follow Gail on the below social media sites and email: <br />Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/AuthorGailMcHugh?ref=hl">https://www.facebook.com/AuthorGailMc...</a><br />Twitter: @Gail_McHugh<br />Amazon: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amazon.com/author/gailmchugh">amazon.com/author/gailmchugh</a><br />Email: author.gail.mchugh@gmail.com <br />And her blog at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.authorgailmchugh.com">www.authorgailmchugh.com</a><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
